					}

				}
			}
			set_temp_variable = { percent_change = 4 }

			change_influence_percentage = yes
			set_temp_variable = { loyalty_change = -0.10 }

				swap_ideas = {
					add_idea = LBA_empowered_peoples_congress
					remove_idea = LBA_general_peoples_congress

					}
